Li Sze-hao Visits Tashiro in Tianjin 81

Exchange of Opinions on Economic Cooperation in North China, Tashiro Expresses Eagerness for Cooperation to Materialize, Li's Observations on Economic Development, Believes Can Indeed Shift Sino-Japanese Political Situation Tianjin Correspondence, Li Sze-hao arrived in Tianjin from Peiping on the afternoon of the 18th around 6:00 PM. On the afternoon of the 19th at 3:00 PM, accompanied by Chen Chueh-sheng, he visited Japanese Commander Tashiro at the Japanese Army Headquarters in Hai Kuang Temple in the Japanese Concession. The discussion lasted two hours. At the time, Chief of Staff of the Japanese Army, Hashimoto, Senior Staff Officer Iida, Staff Officers Kazu, Senda, Adachi, and attached officers Nagamine, Suzuki, etc. were all present. Tashiro introduced them to Li and they exchanged opinions on economic cooperation in North China. Tashiro expressed that the Japanese side is urgently seeking the realization of economic development in North China and hopes that the Chahar-Hopei side can have someone like Mr. Li to be responsible so that progress can be made quickly. In addition to expressing his personal opinions, Li also explained the process by which he accepted the position of Chairman of the Chahar-Hopei Economic Committee. He took his leave at 5:00 PM. Afterwards, he contacted Japanese Consul General Horiuchi by telephone and requested an impromptu meeting. Horiuchi agreed, and he then went to the Japanese Consulate General. According to Horiuchi, the Japanese side has placed its utmost faith in economic cooperation in North China and hopes that it will be realized quickly. He also hopes to promote political stability in North China so that Japanese financial groups can invest without worries. Li took his leave around 6:00 PM. That evening at 7:00 PM, Chen Chueh-sheng hosted a banquet for Mr. Li at the North Ning Residence on Hai Ho Road in the Special Area, inviting Qi Xie-yuan, Wang Yitang, Lu Tsung-yu, etc. to accompany them. Li is scheduled to meet with Tianjin bankers and industrialists on the 20th, return to Peiping on the 21st to report to Song, and go to Nanking around the 25th for consultations, as well as meet with financiers in Shanghai and return north within ten days. It is heard that the Japanese side hopes to emphasize railways, mines, and aviation in the economic development of North China. Although they also hope to realize ports, electricity, Lu salt, and cotton production, they do not have enough capital to invest a large amount at once. Furthermore, financial groups such as Mitsui, Okura, Mitsubishi, etc. are mostly unwilling to be controlled by the army and invest large sums in projects designated by the military. They also feel that the current Japanese military strategy towards China carries the risk of rash action, and that capital investment has no guarantee. Therefore, in order to entice financial groups to join the economic cooperation policy, the Japanese military has reversed its pro-war stance. Senior officers of the Japanese garrison in North China especially want to promote the economic development plan in order to prevent the young officers of the army and navy, who advocate for war in China, from having a pretext. Therefore, the Japanese military in North China has not yet taken active steps to divide and disintegrate the Nanjing diplomacy. The Hsing Chung Company seems to have the same economic policy as the Japanese military on the surface, but in essence, it is still mostly based on the Japanese military's proposals. It probably wants to use the company's detached position to mobilize funds domestically and facilitate the operation of various industries in the development of North China.

At 7:00 PM on the 19th, Li Sze-hao met with Tianjin reporters at the Hotel des Colonies. Before he returned to his residence, he asked Qian Shouyi to entertain them first. Qian then explained Li's itinerary on his behalf. After 7:00 PM, Li returned from the Japanese Consulate General and told the reporters that although the economic development of North China is a local matter, it can indeed shift Sino-Japanese political situation. If this matter can proceed smoothly, it can at least reduce some of the diplomatic burden. The results of my meetings with Tashiro and Horiuchi today were generally very good. It is a pity that Staff Officer Ikeda, the chief of the Third Section in charge of economic affairs in the Japanese military, returned to his country due to an event, and I was unable to talk with him. The key economic development outlines emphasized by the Japanese side, such as cotton production, Lu salt, the construction of the Tianjin-Shijiazhuang Railway, the mining of the Lungyen iron ore, and the organization of aviation, etc., are most eagerly awaited in the Tianjin-Shijiazhuang Railway, aviation, and Lungyen mine. The construction of the Tianjin-Shijiazhuang Railway is determined, but how to start construction has not yet been determined. Today, I and Tashiro and Horiuchi exchanged views on general matters. They did not make any specific expressions. I told them that since we are talking about Sino-Japanese economic cooperation, the first thing to do is to decide how to raise funds. Only with capital can we talk about cooperation. For example, the construction of the Cangzhou-Shijiazhuang Railway requires 20 million yuan, half from China and half from Japan. I asked where the Chahar-Hopei Political Affairs Commission would raise the funds, and it is necessary to allow them to think of a way. There are so many aspects of the economy in North China waiting to be developed. If there is no scope and they are all carried out at the same time, the Chahar-Hopei Political Affairs Commission will feel insufficient in financial resources and manpower. If the Japanese side is willing to show the scale, Song Chairman also has the determination to cooperate, and it can be carried out step by step. Tashiro and Horiuchi quite agreed with this. Therefore, I have decided to wait for Shannan to return and, based on the wishes of all parties, be responsible to Song Chairman to do it, etc. (19th)

Content of the Chahar Northern Puppet Army: Actual Strength No More Than Eight or Nine Thousand, Wang Bandit Splits Into Two Routes to Disturb Sui and Jin 82

Peiping Correspondence, according to reports from relevant parties, the organization of the puppet army in the northern part of Chahar is very large, but the content is extremely empty. The actual strength is no more than eight or nine thousand people, and most of them are a motley crowd. The names are also quite complicated. The pseudo-Mongolian First Army is concurrently commanded by Li Shou-hsin as army commander. The army is divided into four divisions, all of which are cavalry, totaling over five thousand people. The pseudo-Mongolian Second Army is concurrently commanded by Te Wang as army commander, with only two cavalry divisions, each division with three regiments, totaling over two thousand people. Recently, Bao Yue-qing expanded by more than a thousand people in the Duolun area. The pseudo-Anti-Communist Autonomous Army is commanded by Wang Ying, with the army headquarters located in Shangdu City. There are a total of two cavalry brigades, with the first brigade commander being Shi Yu-shan, leading more than a thousand people, and the second brigade commander being Zhao Kuige, leading only three hundred people. The rest are infantry under Li Ying, with no number, and are currently recruiting refugees in the Guyuan area. Those currently confronting the Sui army in the Pingdiquan area on the Chahar-Sui border are the two brigades under Wang Ying. The rest are still preparing to move and are quite busy. Wang Ying's troops have recently been concentrated in Shangdu. Their direction has been determined. They plan to divide their forces into two routes, one from Shangdu to Xinghe, to capture Datong and Fengzhen, and the other from Shangdu to Taolin, to capture Zhuozi Mountain. Heavy weapons have been supplemented within the puppet army, and there are four armored vehicles and several aircraft, all parked in Zhangbei awaiting orders. The situation in the eastern part of Sui is becoming increasingly tense. The Sui authorities have made strict precautions. However, even though the situation is like this, there should be no major changes in the very short term.

Smuggling Ronin Cause Great Disturbance at Jinan Station: The Cause Was the Interception of Smuggled Goods by the Anti-Smuggling Office, Ronin Beat Our Railway Police and Staff, Finally Returning the Smuggled Goods to Resolve the Matter 83

Jinan Correspondence, recently, the wind of smuggling has become very strong again. Because Shandong is adjacent to Hopei Province, and Tianjin is only 700 li away from Jinan, the number of smuggled goods transported by automobiles to Jinan, Zhoucun and other places is no less than sixty to seventy vehicles every day. Most of them are white sugar, cigarette paper, rayon, etc. On the morning of the 18th, the Tianjin Anti-Smuggling Office stationed in Jinan, which is authorized to prohibit road transportation smuggling by the Ministry of Finance, seized two automobiles of smuggled rayon, cigarette paper, and white sugar, and transported the smuggled goods to the goods factory of Jinpu Station, loaded into cars, and transported to Beijing. Unexpectedly, at 7:00 PM, a group of 70-80 smuggling ronin suddenly gathered at the station to cause trouble. With great momentum, they first surrounded the cargo room. Because the office staff there had escaped in advance, only the duty policeman Jin Ju-wen was on the scene and was beaten. Patrol Captain Yang Yu-zhi rushed to persuade them to stop, but he was also beaten and humiliated. They caused trouble back and forth in the station, and the order was in great disorder. All the anti-smuggling office personnel escaped. Staff Liu Mao-zhi was unable to escape and was caught by the ronin, dragged to the south platform of the cargo factory, and beaten with fists and feet, followed by sticks. Liu was unable to move at the time, lying on the platform, crying and wailing in a very miserable voice. At this time, the station employees also stayed far away, and no one dared to come forward to persuade them to stop. Many onlookers were also beaten and humiliated. The ronin then dragged Liu Mao-zhi to the anti-smuggling office, forced him to call the China Travel Service, and forced the person in charge of customs to come to the station and hand over the goods. Director Lin Le-ming also avoided coming to the station. Liu held the telephone, weeping and shouting, saying that if he did not come again, his life would not be guaranteed, etc. The ronin who transported the goods then tightly closed Liu in the room. At this time, the Public Security Bureau heard the news, fearing that it would cause trouble, and immediately sent Inspector Li De-qin along with the consultant of the bureau, Kageshita (Japanese), to the station to mediate. They discussed with the person in charge of the Japanese Police Station. As a result, the anti-smuggling office handed over the goods, and then the Japanese side released Liu Mao-zhi. The Public Security Bureau then invited the staff of the anti-smuggling office, Zhang Jia-kun and Gao Zhong-qi, to the station to discuss the matter face to face. When the Chinese and Japanese sides were about to prepare for negotiations in the first-class waiting room, the smuggling ronin broke into the living room and brutally beat Zhang Jia-kun and Gao Zhong-qi. Railway police and public security bureau personnel were unable to dissuade them. Gao and Zhang were both bleeding from their heads. At this point, the ronin became more and more proud, and shouted and strode out of the living room, still surrounding and refusing to leave. Negotiations lasted until late at night, and as a result, the goods were left in Tai'an, transported back to Jinan on the 19th, and handed over to the Japanese consulate for disposal. The dispute was resolved. (18th)

Ronin Sneak into Chao-Shan to Spy, Strange Warships Patrol Nanao Island, Swatow City is Full of Han Traitor Organizations, Japanese Women and Children in Swatow Return to Taiwan One After Another 84

Swatow Correspondence, since the discovery of the discarded bombs in Kwong Tze 洋行 on the night of September 17, China and Japan have repeatedly studied the discarded bombs, and found many suspicious points. The responsibility issue has not yet been determined. However, the Japanese Consul stationed in Swatow has made a request to the municipal government, according to the resolution of the Japanese residents' conference, to arrest and punish the culprits, protect Japanese residents, and completely eliminate the anti-Japanese movement. Originally, there was a Japanese warship Akikaze berthed in Swatow Port. Since then, another Uzuki has arrived. Recently, Akikaze left Swatow and was replaced by Fuyou. There are always two Japanese warships on alert in the waters of Swatow. However, according to fishermen in Nanao who came to Swatow, recently there have often been ronin going to Nanao to survey the surrounding fortresses and photograph the terrain. Three or five people form a group. They do not notify our police authorities in advance to protect them. After entering the country, they gallop around without any scruples. In the past five days, there have been faster ships and submarines without national flags patrolling around Nanao Island. The submarine is No. 11, and its whereabouts are unusually secretive. Ronin have also been repeatedly discovered in the inland areas of Chaoan, Chaoyang, Chenghai, and Raoping counties, specializing in taking pictures of river banks, harbors, docks, markets, and other important defense points. Some also pretend to be medicine sellers, selling medicines and children's toys at low prices, and go to various villages, looking around, sometimes staying in food stores and opium dens. The purpose they hold is self-evident. It is heard that since September, no fewer than two to three hundred people have been newly dispatched to work deep inland, and their urgency can be imagined.

Since the discovery of the discarded bomb case at Kwong Tze 洋行 in Swatow City, the Public Security Bureau has tightened martial law, and armed military police are stationed at posts, with one soldier every five steps and one sentry every ten steps. Unemployed vagrants, hooligans, and so-called suspects in the city have been arrested by the dozens. According to a certain intelligence report, secret organizations of Han traitors are scattered throughout the city's key points. In certain warehouses in Kwong Wah 埠, Wu Bridge side, etc., which are farther from the city, ronin often gather late at night, and ronin use small boats to transport heavy wooden boxes into the warehouses. Therefore, people's hearts are frightened and the atmosphere is serious. On the 12th and 13th, dozens of Japanese women and children took advantage of the Japanese ships Hong Kong Maru and Fengshan Maru bound for Taiwan to go to Taiwan. Japanese primary schools have virtually suspended classes. Therefore, rumors in Swatow City are becoming more and more prevalent. Fortunately, the military police are strictly guarded, so the market is as peaceful as usual. (16th)

Shengsi Islands Still Under Jiangsu Province Jurisdiction; Executive Yuan Instructions Have Arrived in Jiangsu, Resolving the Dispute Between the Two Provinces 85

Zhenjiang Dispatch: The case of the boundary dispute over the Shengsi Islands between Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces was forwarded by the Executive Yuan to the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Interior, and the Ministry of Industry, as well as the governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, for review. Each party held its own opinion, so the case was submitted to President Chiang for a ruling. It was decided that the Shengsi Islands would remain under the jurisdiction of Jiangsu Province. The instructions from the Executive Yuan have already arrived in the province and have been forwarded by the provincial government to the Nantong commissioner for notification. The text of the Executive Yuan's instructions to the Jiangsu Provincial Government is as follows: "Regarding the Shengsi Islands boundary issue, the case was previously submitted to your provincial government, the Zhejiang Provincial Government, the Ministry of Interior, the Ministry of Finance, and the Ministry of Industry for joint review. According to the reported review results, the Jiangsu Province representative proposed a boundary at 30 degrees 32 minutes north latitude (i.e., keeping the Shengsi Islands under Jiangsu's administration). The Zhejiang Province representative advocated a boundary at 30 degrees 52 minutes north latitude (i.e., assigning the Shengsi Islands to Zhejiang's administration). The representatives from the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry advocated maintaining the status quo (i.e., keeping the Shengsi Islands under Jiangsu's administration). The representative from the Ministry of Interior advocated implementing the two resolutions previously decided upon at the Ministry's meetings: (1) All of Dahuanglong Island and Xiaohuanglong Island should be placed under the jurisdiction of Zhejiang Province. Tanhu Mountain and Baishan should be placed under the jurisdiction of Jiangsu Province. The boundary lines of all coastal islands of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces should uniformly follow the original boundary lines on the military maps prepared by the Army Survey Bureau. (2) Based on this resolution, the Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Industry should jointly consult with the Jiangsu and Zhejiang provincial governments, and after consultation and reply, the matter should be submitted to the Executive Yuan for record in accordance with departmental regulations.) Each party held its own reasoning, and a resolution was submitted for the President's approval. Therefore, the status quo should be maintained, with the Islands remaining under the jurisdiction of Jiangsu Province. In addition to instructing the Zhejiang Provincial Government to comply, the Ministry of Interior, the Ministry of Finance, and the Ministry of Industry are also hereby notified."

Suzhou: Butcher Knife Injures Axe Gang Member 86

Yao Fuqing, who operates a woodworking shop near the Xiguan Bridge in the city, had a feud with Xu A'da, a member of the Axe Gang. On the 19th, around 8 PM, Xu A'da, along with his followers Tang Guochang, Yang Longhai, and others, encountered Yao Fuqing. Xu immediately attacked Yao and his partner Yu Dabao with an axe. Yao, also prepared, took out a butcher knife and quickly slashed Xu A'da twice in the back. At that time, both Yu Dabao and Xu A'da were injured and fell to the ground. The rest of the gang immediately dispersed, and Yao also fled without a trace. The police arrived and sent the injured to Guangmin Hospital for treatment. However, Xu A'da's injuries were the most severe and life-threatening. The responsible police district took Yao Fuqing's wife, Wang, to the district and sent her to the branch bureau for questioning. They are also searching for Yao Fuqing to bring him to justice.

Changshu: Bust of Opium Trafficking Organization 87

According to a report, the County Public Security Bureau busted an illegal opium trafficking organization outside the Southeast Gate on the 19th. The mastermind was Fang Desheng, the former patrol officer of the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau. The organization was tightly structured and difficult for outsiders to detect. A minor internal conflict led to a secret report. After the Public Security Bureau's Inspectorate received the report, they first arrested Qian Yongchun at a cigarette paper shop outside the South Gate and seized twelve packages of opium. Based on Qian's confession, they then searched the home of the mastermind, Fang Desheng, and found some illegal opium, as well as three letters in his pillow that were strongly related to the illegal opium trade. Both the people and the evidence were taken to the county. Fang claimed that he only smoked the opium himself and did not sell it privately. The investigation is ongoing. Fang is from Hebei, 48 years old, and has served as a patrol officer and branch bureau chief in various branches of the public security sector. Recently, when the new Director Chen was transferred to Changshu, Fang was excluded. Because he had been in Changshu for over ten years and did not want to leave, he took this risky action.

Wuxi: Eight-County Air Defense Drill 88

The Wuxi, Wu, and Kunshan counties will jointly conduct a large-scale air defense drill in early November with the eight counties of the second district of Jiangsu Province: Wuxi, Wujin, Jiangyin, Wuxian, Wujiang, Changshu, Kunshan, and Taicang. The air defense units in this county have already been organized and include the Public Security Bureau, the Traffic Control Brigade, the Construction Bureau's Engineering Brigade, the Sixth Security Brigade's Garrison Brigade, the Firefighting Joint Association's Fire Brigade, and the Medical Association's Ambulance Brigade. The candidates for the heads of all the brigades have also been determined. These units will now be reorganized into defense regiments.

Tangkou Opens New Salt Field 89

The Liuhe Salt Field, established by Central Committee member Zhang Jingjiang, is quite large in scale. The salt used by salt merchants north and south of the Yangtze River is purchased from this field. Recently, feeling that the original field was insufficient, it was decided to select a site of more than 50 mu on the edge of the Goose-and-Duck Lake in Tangkou Town, the eighth district of this county, to build a new salt field. The funds were a loan of one million yuan in salt tax from the Ministry of Finance. Construction began a month ago and is now complete. The salt stored in the field is enough to supply the people of Jiangsu Province for three years. In recent days, a large number of laborers have been hired in Wuxi to transport salt to Liuhe in preparation for relocation. Zhang has also enclosed more than 100 mu of farmland in Jintan to build a Zhejiang salt warehouse. A small portion of the buildings has now been completed, and the rest will be built next spring. It is said that its scale is more than double that of the Tangkou Salt Field.

Changzhou: Approval of Deed Tax and Surcharges 90

The deed tax surcharge in Wujin County was repeatedly ordered to be reduced in the past. Recently, the county government explained the circumstances that made further reductions impossible. The Ministry of Finance approved a temporary collection of two yuan and two jiao per hundred yuan of deed value from property owners by the Deed Tax Office for educational funding, deleting the original fraction of six li and seven hao, and issuing receipts. The fractional amounts of six jiao, six fen, and seven li of the original construction surcharge and local surcharge were also waived, and only six jiao per hundred yuan of deed value was allowed to be collected. A public announcement must be widely published and posted on thoroughfares so that the people are fully informed.

Gaoyou: Large Fire in a Farmer's Home in Xinyi Township 91

The home of Wang Youjiang, a farmer in Beishahu, Xinyi Township, the seventh district of Huxi, caught fire around 7 PM on the 17th when his wife, being careless while lighting a lamp, overturned the kerosene tank. The fire broke out instantly, and the woman was engulfed in flames. By the time her family pulled her out, the fire had spread to the house. In an instant, the fire lit up the sky and could not be extinguished. It wasn't until 11 PM that the fire was put out. All 18 rooms of the house, 30 dan of stored wheat, more than 100 dan of rice, and all clothing and utensils were reduced to ashes. 100+ legal tender was also burned. The total loss is estimated to be more than 4,000 yuan. Wang's wife suffered severe burns, with her eyebrows and hair completely gone, and her life is feared to be in danger.

Strange Occurrence: Apricot Trees Bloom Out of Season 92

The apricot tree in front of the ancestral hall of the Gong family, residents of West Back Street in the city, has suddenly bloomed a second time, causing a sensation throughout the city. Everyone who goes to see it marvels at its strangeness. Unexpectedly, the apricot tree in the home of Xue Wenpo, who runs a fish shop in Lingqiao Town, the seventh district of Huxi, is also blooming. The color is bright and vivid, no different from those that bloom in the spring. Many people from nearby villages are going to see it.

Yangzhou: Kongjiagou Organizes River Dredging Association 93

The Kongjiagou River is located at the junction of the fourth and seventh districts. Due to river dredging, a dispute once arose. The heads of the fourth and seventh districts jointly submitted a request to the county government for instructions. The county government instructed the organization of a river dredging committee to handle the matter. The committee has now been established, with Zhu Hetang and others elected as executive members and Zhou Jinzhang and others as supervisory members. They are scheduled to be sworn in on October 26 to carry out water conservancy work. The fourth and seventh districts have reported to the county for record.

Funing: Air Defense Drill Held 94

Wang Baoquan, the principal of the central public school in the first district of this county, reported to County Magistrate Wang Shuxian on the 17th that the first class of trained young men at the school will soon graduate. In order to implement air defense drills, the county government issued a notice for light control. Firstly, the power company was instructed to turn off the lights at 8 PM on the 18th. All the young men from the school were deployed to patrol the streets and alleys, with local military police also participating in the drill. At the designated time, thousands of lights went out simultaneously, and it was quiet and silent. At 8:45 PM, the lights were restored. The results were quite good.

Huzhou: Carelessness at Dacheng Paper Store 95

The fourth warehouse of the Dacheng Paper Goods Store in Tuoluo Bridge, near the river, caught fire suddenly around 10:30 PM on the 18th. Firefighters from various districts rushed to put out the fire, which burned for half an hour before being extinguished. As a result, four warehouse rooms were burned down.

Yuyao: Large Fire in Sanguan Township 96

The Yitaixing Flower Shop in Tanheyan, Sanguan Township, Yuyao, is jointly operated by Mao Qinong, Du Youxiang, Sun Yatang, and others. The business is thriving and profitable. It is currently the cotton harvest season, and more than 30,000 catties of cotton have been collected and stored in the shop. Unexpectedly, around 10 PM on the 16th, a worker at the shop accidentally knocked over a kerosene lamp onto a pile of cotton. The fire ignited instantly, and because everything was flammable, and the fire was extremely intense, it could not be extinguished. After burning for more than two hours, the fire was finally extinguished by the efforts of the crowd. However, more than 30 rooms of the shop, more than 30,000 catties of cotton, and all the account books were reduced to ashes. The manager's head was burned in the fire. The total loss is estimated to be more than 20,000 yuan.

Ningbo: Second Air Defense Drill 97

The second large-scale air defense drill in the urban area was officially held on the 18th. Due to six days of intensive publicity, the people had a much better understanding of air defense knowledge, and the order was quite good. At 12:05 PM, after receiving a warning that enemy aircraft were invading from Hangzhou, a state of alert was immediately declared throughout the city. All air defense units were dispatched to defend. At 2:35 PM, six aircraft were over Ningbo. The sirens of various factories sounded simultaneously, and the alarm bell on the drum tower also rang loudly. All traffic was blocked, and shops closed their doors and suspended business. The atmosphere was tense. It wasn't until 3:40 PM, when the enemy aircraft had moved far away, that normalcy was restored. In the evening, a simulated night air raid alert was received, and a light control was implemented. All the lights in the city were extinguished, and a special curfew was imposed. People all took shelter and did not come out. After 10 PM, the lights were restored. This drill was well organized and the results of the advance publicity had a positive effect, making the process good and better than last time.

Hangzhou: Request to Allocate Funds for Repairing Dangerous Dikes 98

The Zhejiang Construction Department believes that the Gongmao character-numbered dikes of the Hai dike on the Hangzhou-Ping section are in danger due to the outward movement of the dike body. It has specially sent Zhou Zhenlun, the director of the Water Conservancy Engineering Office, to inspect the results. In addition to the two dikes, many other dangerous dike works have been found, all of which need to be repaired. Surveyors have been sent to measure the site, prepare a budget of the necessary engineering expenses, and submit a request to the provincial government for a special disaster relief fund of 30,000 to 40,000 yuan to start repairing the dangerous dikes.

Financial Department Borrows One Million 99

In order to meet the needs of government expenses and raise funds for the principal and interest of public bonds, the Zhejiang Financial Department is borrowing one million yuan from the Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications. After contacting the responsible persons of the three banks, they are now separately requesting instructions from their respective headquarters in Shanghai. The interest rates, collateral, and repayment period are still under negotiation and should be established and signed next month. It is said that the Central Bank and the Bank of China will each provide 400,000 yuan, while the Bank of Communications will provide 200,000 yuan.

Nantong: Squeezing Out Arrears of Past Taxes 100

Tong County has a total of more than 2.3 million yuan in outstanding farmland taxes from previous years. A committee for collecting arrears of taxes has been jointly formed by various agencies, using the baojia system to squeeze out the taxes. In order to avoid affecting the new taxes, the system of top-offs and strings has been abolished. For farmland that has collapsed into the river, after verifying the deeds, requests to the province for exemption are permitted. Caiyang, Henghe, and Xinchang townships in Wenling's eastern district have been ordered to recruit young men for training and are proceeding accordingly. On the 16th, misunderstandings arose among the villagers of these three townships. The crowd rioted at the homes of the township chiefs and destroyed property. After receiving the report, the county government immediately dispatched a team to investigate and advised the villagers.

Huaiyin: County Party Headquarters Advocates Mountain Climbing 101

The County Party Headquarters of this county is promoting mountain climbing during the Double Ninth Festival. It specially convened a meeting of people from all walks of life to prepare, and the following matters were decided: (1) It will be named the Huaiyin Public Double Ninth Festival Mountain Climbing Movement. (2) The location will follow tradition and will still be the Yuwang Palace, which is the West Park of the city. (3) The arrangements at that time will be as follows: A. Display of various chrysanthemums; B. Holding of singing tea houses; C. Display of antiques and calligraphy; D. Folk custom exhibitions; E. Establishment of a book market; F. Costume propaganda. Among them, the fourth item will be the responsibility of the Provincial Public Education Hall, the fifth item will be the responsibility of the Public Security Bureau, and the rest will be the responsibility of the Party Headquarters. As for the date, it will be set for the 23rd of this month, and the County Party Headquarters will issue a notice in advance to people from all walks of life to participate at that time.

Recent Situation in Guangdong and Guangxi (7) 102

— Our Reporter Xiao'an

Guangzhou's Municipal Administration (Continued)

Regarding the matters of the Finance Bureau: (1) Abolishing the contractor system: In Guangzhou City, various taxes and levies have mostly adopted a contractor system. After contractors bid, they pay the treasury on schedule, and the city treasury has a fixed income, without the worry of sudden increases or decreases. However, merchants must have profits to be willing to engage in it; otherwise, no one will bid. Even if the reserve price is sharply reduced and the date is repeatedly changed, they will still wait and see. The Finance Bureau now intends to change all taxes and levies to delegated management, making them easier to organize and hoping to increase tax revenue. (2) Reducing the burden on citizens: Many taxes and levies in Guangzhou are attached with a surcharge. For example, the rickshaw tax rate is high, and overdue land taxes have penalty interest. In order to reduce the burden on citizens, the Finance Bureau is reducing and exempting these taxes separately. (3) Raising funds to repay accumulated debts: The Guangzhou City education fund has accumulated more than 500,000 yuan in debt due to insufficient treasury funds. The Finance Bureau is now planning to raise funds and repay the debts in succession. Other debts are also being resolved and cleaned up. (4) Completing the Inner Harbor Plan: The construction of Guangzhou City's inner harbor has not yet been completed. The Finance Bureau plans to continue construction to facilitate transportation and increase revenue. (5) Opening up new residential areas: Guangzhou City has a vast area and dense buildings, which is known for its prosperity. However, there are few residences suitable for hygiene. The Finance Bureau is now planning to open up several residential areas to tidy up the city appearance and improve people's health.

Regarding the matters of the Public Works Bureau: (1) Opening up important trunk roads in the suburbs of the city; (2) Resuming the construction of roads in the city that have been suspended; (3) Constructing Haizhu Embankment Road and various cross-roads; (4) Planning and constructing City Center Road; (5) Opening up inner streets and improving street surfaces; (6) Repairing existing road surfaces; (7) Continuing the construction of the Southwest Railway Bridge; (8) Continuing the construction of the Xinbinhua Bridge; (9) Continuing the construction of various bridges in Donghao; (10) Continuing the construction of the downstream project of Donghao; (11) Reconstructing inner street canals; (12) Cleaning up various moats and inner street canals; (13) Cleaning up road canals; (14) Continuing the construction of the municipal government joint office; (15) Continuing the construction of the municipal hospital; (16) Constructing a storage room for the municipal government joint office; (17) Continuing the construction of the Henan embankment; (18) Rectifying the business of the automobile company; (19) Strictly examining automobile driving talents; (20) Improving and adding parking lots throughout the city; (21) Planning for trolleybuses; (22) Improving the lives of rickshaw drivers; (23) Rectifying the city-run cross-sea electric boats; (24) Rectifying the electrical equipment in public places; (25) Rectifying traffic lights and watchtowers.

Regarding the matters of the Electricity Department: (1) Rectifying various projects; (2) Rectifying business matters; (3) Rectifying accounting matters.

Regarding the matters of the Telephone Association: (1) Rectifying the Foshan branch and the provincial-Foshan long-distance telephone line; (2) Repairing the machine factory and materials; (3) Adding the number of internal telephone numbers in the general and branch offices.

Regarding the matters of the Waterworks Department: (1) Improving household registration; (2) Increasing water volume and clarifying water quality; (3) Organizing an investigation team; (4) Relocating the chemical laboratory; (5) Constructing a material warehouse; (6) Clearing up old debts; (7) Strictly investigating water theft; (8) Reconstructing street pipes.

Regarding the matters of the Sewerage Engineering Department: Every year in Guangzhou City, there are floods whenever there is heavy rain. Therefore, the Sewerage Engineering Department was established to rectify this. The projects that have been determined by the department are: (1) Rectifying the upstream of Donghao; (2) Rectifying the Six Meridian canals; (3) Rectifying the Yudaihao and Xihongyong; (4) Building a tidal gate in West City.

The above items are the central work newly determined by the municipal government, and efforts are being made to actively implement them. In addition, there are also the Municipal Bank, the Municipal Library, and the Municipal Museum. The municipal government is also making new plans for them. As for the newly established agencies of the municipal government, there are the New Life Movement Promotion Association and the Municipal Anti-Smoking Committee. All efforts are being made. After taking office as mayor, Zeng Yangfu made a speech, roughly saying, "Guangzhou is not only the most important area in Guangdong Province, but also the hub of China's politics and economy and the birthplace of the revolution. Therefore, Guangzhou's municipal administration is extremely important. I believe that the various measures taken by the municipal administration in the past have not met the standards. Compared with Nanjing, Shanghai, Hangzhou, Tianjin, Hankou, and other cities, they are all behind. After taking office, I am determined to make major rectifications, cut redundant personnel who waste public funds, eliminate various long-standing malpractices, and eradicate corruption, so that official governance can be clarified. On the one hand, increase funding for affairs and construction, follow the instructions of the central and provincial governments, do my best, and rely on public opinion to realize the plan to build a new Guangzhou." From this statement, it can be seen that Zeng has a clear understanding of Guangzhou and his determination to work hard on Guangzhou's municipal administration. Because of this understanding and determination, he has selected people he trusts to serve as directors of the various bureaus and committees under the municipal government, such as Liu Shixin, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau; Mai Jianzeng, Director of the Finance Bureau; Zeng Qian, Director of the Land Bureau; Ouyang Cong, Director of the Health Bureau; Lin Yimin, Director of the Public Works Bureau; as well as Zeng Qian, Secretary-General of the Municipal Government; Chen Shaoxian and Li Fang, Secretaries; Liang Bingxian, Huang Shiguang, Qiu Heqing, and Li Zaojian, Councilors. Also, the Public Utilities Bureau was merged into the Public Works Bureau, the Education Bureau was merged into the Social Affairs Bureau, and the new power plant was merged into the Electricity Management Office. Previously, the municipal government had a total of seven bureaus and two power plants; now there are five bureaus and one office. The scope of the agency seems to have shrunk, but the affairs have not been slackened. In addition, the personnel of various bureaus and offices have been reduced by a considerable amount. It is said that nearly 100 employees have been replaced in the Waterworks Management Office alone. The staff of other bureaus and committees have also been changed. This is all to put Zeng's words of major rectification and elimination of malpractices into practice.

Instructions for Referees

Instructions for officials and referees of the Games: (1) The Games office is located in the auditorium at the north end of the West Commander's Platform; (2) The referees' rest area is on the West Commander's Platform; (3) The Secretary-General's office is located in the stadium director's office at the south end of the West Commander's Platform; (4) The Games lunch time is from 12:00 noon every day; (5) Referees' refreshments will be served at 3:30 PM every day in the referees' rest area; (6) The Games canteen is located in the bullet room at the north end of the West Commander's Platform.

Pick-up Locations

Locations for vehicles picking up and dropping off referees: (1) Wushu referees gather at the Municipal Wushu Hall in New Zhabei, with Zhu Wenwei responsible for hiring a Cheung Shing taxi; the second gathering point is Lu Xun Road, East Asia Physical Education College, with Sun Hebin responsible; the third gathering point is Renji Road, Municipal No. 1 Stadium, with Shen Xian responsible; the fourth gathering point is the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA, with Chen Dongbai responsible; the fifth gathering point is the Sichuan Road YMCA, with Gan Fengxiang responsible. Each person in charge is responsible for hiring a Cheung Shing taxi to take them to the venue. Other referees, such as those from West Shanghai, can gather on their own and hire a Cheung Shing taxi to go to the Games. All transportation expenses can be claimed from Yuan Zengyu at the information desk on the West Commander's Platform.

Opening Ceremony Order

(1) Opening (Music); (2) Officials and athletes parade around the field; (3) All stand at attention to raise the Games flag; (4) Sing the Party song; (5) Offer the highest respect to the Party, national flag, and portrait of Sun Yat-sen; (6) A representative reads Sun Yat-sen's last will and testament; (7) The chairman delivers the opening address; (8) Athletes take the oath; (9) The mayor delivers instructions; (10) The Party representative delivers instructions; (11) Music concludes the ceremony (athletes leave the field); (12) Mass drill performance.

Key Points for the Parade

Key points for the athletes' parade: 1. By 9:00 AM on October 22nd, all groups of athletes should gather on the cinder path south of the east gate of the track and field, outside the gate, and form a line to await departure. 2. The order of the parade is as follows: (1) Social Affairs Bureau band; (2) Games officials, referees, and athletes (A) Middle school group, high school in front, junior high behind; (B) University group; (C) Physical education school group; (D) Open group; (E) Wushu group; (3) Athletes and officials of each group should line up in a four-column formation according to the above order, with officials of each group in front of the athletes of each group, female athletes in front, and male athletes behind. (4) The Games will provide a unit flag for each group as a symbol, and each group will select one athlete to hold it and lead the way. (5) After entering through the east gate, each group turns right and parades around the field along the track. When passing in front of the West Commander's Platform, all officials and athletes must turn right and salute. They then turn into the center of the field at the southeast corner and proceed towards the West Commander's Platform. Each group then turns towards the Commander's Platform one by one and stops five meters from the track. (6) During the parade, all officials of each group must wear uniforms and are not allowed to wear long robes. All athletes must wear clean and tidy sportswear. (7) During the parade, there should be eight steps between each group and four steps between officials and athletes within each group. There should be two steps between each small row, and they should not be too far apart or too close together. (8) Games officials and referees do not need to continue forward after passing in front of the Commander's Platform. (9) After the ceremony, they should return to the outside of the East Commander's Platform in the original order and disperse.

Oath Ceremony

Oath ceremony for athletes: (1) An appointed representative will take the oath; (2) When the representative slowly steps onto the oath platform, the unit flags of each group will advance with them and form a semi-circular formation in front of the oath platform, with the flags facing forward; (3) The representative bows to the Commander's Platform, and all athletes stand at attention at the same time; (4) The representative raises their right hand and silently recites the oath; (5) When taking the oath, the unit flags of each group should tilt forward to perform the flag salute; (6) After the representative finishes reading the oath, they bow and step down from the oath platform, and the unit flags of each group step back to their original positions; (7) Oath: We hereby uphold the spirit of physical education advocated by Sun Yat-sen, participate in the competition as amateur athletes, obey the referees, and abide by all the rules of the Games. This we swear.

Mass Drill Formation

(1) Each team consists of fifty people, arranged in a column; (2) The team leaders of each school stand in front of each squad; (3) When entering the field in formation, the students in each squad should be arranged with shorter students in front and taller students in the back; (4) Four squads line up side by side and enter the field in a single file of four columns; (5) After entering the field and parading, each squad arranges itself according to the prescribed layout, from east to west, smallest in front, largest in back, facing the West Commander's Platform, and enters and organizes itself in order, standing on the symbol of each performing position on the field; (6) Cheering: All students pick up the performing symbol from the position they are standing on with their right hand; (7) When cheering, raise your right hand, with the symbol still held in your right hand.

Detailed Record of the Annual Meeting of the Chinese Cooperative Society (Part 2): Discussed Cooperative Guidance Technology, Passed Over 30 Important Cases 109

Central Issues Discussed Item by Item The third general meeting discussed the central issues, chaired by Shou Miancheng. After reporting on the group discussions and the consolidation process, the discussion began, A. General Cooperative Guidance Technology Discussion Outline: (1) System Issues, (2) Education Issues, (3) Organization Issues, (4) Accounting Issues, (5) Business Issues. After item-by-item discussion, amendments, and passage, it was agreed to add insurance business. B. Production Cooperation Guidance Technology Discussion Outline: (1) Production Cooperatives That Should Be Promoted, (2) Steps to Promote Production Cooperatives, (3) Guidance Technology on the Organization of Production Cooperatives, (4) Guidance Technology on the Business of Production Cooperatives. After item-by-item discussion, amendments, and passage. C. Consumer Cooperation Guidance Technology Discussion Outline: (1) Regarding Organizers, (2) Regarding Staff, (3) Regarding the Training of Members, (4) Regarding Business Policies, (5) Regarding Purchasing, (6) Regarding the Storage and Display of Goods, (7) Regarding Sales, (8) Regarding the Invoice System, (9) Regarding Funding, (10) Regarding Profits. After item-by-item discussion, amendments, and passage. D. Credit Cooperation Guidance Technology Discussion Outline: (1) Guidance, (2) Organization, (3) Society Affairs, (4) Business, (5) Non-Economic Activities. After item-by-item discussion, amendments, and passage. Afterwards, the chairman proposed a motion to elect a consolidation committee, which was resolved to be handed over to the next executive committee for consolidation. The meeting then adjourned.

Discussed Proposals, Read Papers The fourth general meeting discussed society affairs proposals and read papers, chaired by He Yushu. This general meeting received a total of 29 society affairs proposals and 9 suggestions. Except for 17 cases that were not related to society affairs, which were separately incorporated into the central issues of each group by the editorial board and the suggestions were resolved to be handed over to the next executive committee for reference and implementation, the remaining 12 cases were: (1) Organizing a memorial meeting for the tenth anniversary of Mr. Xue Xianzhou's death, (2) Organizing a cooperative advisory committee, (3) Initiating a national cooperative association, (4) Joining the International Cooperative Alliance, (5) Using a second language to send cooperative communications, (6) Requesting the determination of fund-raising methods, (7) Establishing a cooperative youth department, (8) Requesting that the next general meeting be held in Sichuan, (9) Drafting the society's implementation outline, (10) Developing the China Cooperative Wholesale Department, (11) Establishing researchers, (12) Creating cooperative codes, (13) Electing fund committee members. Except for the 13th case, which was originally extracted from the 6th case to elect Wen Qun as a committee member, and the 11th case, which was merged into the 9th case, the 6th case resolved that the fund committee should actively handle it. The 7th case required amending Article 13 of the society's charter. The 8th case pre-selected four locations: Guangdong, Sichuan, Beiping, and Jiangxi. All other cases were handed over to the next executive committee for handling. In addition, there were temporary motions: (1) Requesting to send a telegram of condolence to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek in the name of the general meeting, (2) Requesting to send a telegram to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek stating that promoting the cooperative cause is a method for developing the national economy and construction, (3) Requesting to thank the Hunan Provincial Government and various agencies in the name of the general meeting, which were resolved and passed. As for the papers, they included: 1. Wu Yuzhang's "Cooperation and Tenant Farmers Amidst the National Economic Construction Movement," 2. Xu Yuekun's "Adjustment of Rural Idle Funds and Credit Cooperation," 3. Xie Yunzhuang's "Accounting System for Cooperative Warehouses," 4. Pan Chengshi's "Brief Discussion on Rural Cooperative Guidance Technology," 5. Chen Yansong's "Special Problems in Rural Marketing Cooperative Management," 6. Wang Shiying's "Prospects for the Chinese Cooperative Movement," etc. Generous Hospitality from the Hunan Provincial Government The Hunan Provincial Government Construction Department established a reception office for the annual meeting of the Chinese Cooperative Society in Changsha, providing accommodation at the two major hotels, the Traffic Hotel and the Six Nations Hotel, and holding the meeting at the Zhongshan Hall of the Provincial Education Association. In addition to participating in the opening ceremony of the Central China Games, they also invited guests to visit Mount Heng in Nanyue, providing transportation both ways. All members felt very welcome.

False Fengtian Province: Detailed Statistics on Enslavement Education; 5,838 Primary and Secondary Schools; Approximately 470,000 Youths Being Drugged 110

(Northeast News Agency, Shenyang) The Education Department of the false Fengtian Provincial Government, in order to complete the enslavement education throughout the province and to please the Japanese, recently implemented a detailed statistical analysis of education throughout the false province. It distributed a printed overview of education in the entire false province to various agencies and organizations so that Japanese and puppet officials in various regions could understand the situation of the enslavement education facilities in the false Fengtian Province. The statistics and facilities of the false Education Department are recorded as follows:

Situation of Primary and Secondary Schools: There are a total of 5,838 primary and secondary schools, 9,981 classes, 11,688 teachers and staff, and 466,964 students in the entire false province, accounting for more than 44% of all students in the four northeastern provinces.

Comparison of Male and Female Students: There are 810 kindergarten students, with males accounting for over 67% and females accounting for slightly less than 33%. There are 393,286 primary school students, with males accounting for over 77% and females accounting for slightly less than 23%. There are 12,584 secondary school students, with males accounting for over 80% and females accounting for slightly less than 20%. There are 3,704 normal school students, with males accounting for over 68% and females accounting for slightly less than 32%. There are 1,622 vocational students, with males accounting for 76% and females accounting for 24%.

Enrollment Rate: School-age children account for slightly less than 14% of the entire false province's population, and enrolled children account for slightly less than 34% of the number of school-age children. 66% are out of school.

Education Funding This Year: In order to please Japan, pro-Japanese enslavement education has been actively promoted this year, so the funding has reached 6 million yuan, an increase of 2 million yuan compared to the previous year.

Wang Chonghui, Sun Ke, Xu Chongzhi Depart South by Ship This Morning; Ju Zheng Aborts Trip Due to Official Business; Shi Ying and Jiao Yitang Accompany; Wu Kaixian, Representative of the City Party Headquarters, Also on Board; City Chamber of Commerce Dispatches Representative Luo Qinghua Today; Central Government Representative to Pay Respects to Hu 113

Wang Chonghui, a member of the Central Committee specially appointed by the Central Government to attend the state funeral of the late Chairman Hu of the Standing Committee in Guangdong to pay respects; Sun Ke, President of the Legislative Yuan; and Xu Chongzhi, Vice President of the Supervisory Yuan, were scheduled to depart Shanghai this morning at 11:00 AM aboard the Norddeutscher Lloyd ship "Breslau". It was reported that Ju Zheng, President of the Judicial Yuan, was unable to travel due to important official duties. Chen Lifu, a member of the Standing Committee of the Central Committee, had no confirmed information. The ship was anchored on the Jiangmian River at Buoy No. 11 and No. 12 in the Huangpu River. Mr. Sun and others were scheduled to take a specially prepared small customs boat "Jinghui" from the Customs Pier this morning at 9:00 AM to cross the river and board the ship. At that time, Mayor Wu Tiecheng of this city, Songhu Garrison Commander Yang Hu, and others from all parties will go to the ship to bid farewell. It was also learned that Shi Ying, the Minister of Selection of the Examination Yuan and the Ministry of Personnel, and Jiao Yitang, the President of the Supreme Court, and Luo Gang, the representative of the Central Propaganda Department, had already arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing yesterday and were all on the ship. In addition, Wu Kaixian, a member of the Central Committee and a member of the Municipal Supervisory Committee, will also take the ship as a representative of the City Party Headquarters to travel with Sun and Xu.

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, in view of the fact that the state funeral of the late Chairman Hu is scheduled for the 25th of this month, specially appointed Supervisory Committee member Luo Qinghua as a representative to go to Guangdong to pay respects. Mr. Luo was scheduled to depart at 9:00 AM on the 21st from the Customs Pier to board the Breslau mail ship to Guangdong. The memorial text is recorded as follows: Six months after the death of Chairman Hu Gongzhan of the Standing Committee of the Central Executive Committee, the country commemorates the elders and holds a state funeral in Guangzhou. From government offices to mass organizations, representatives are sent to attend the funeral to express condolences. Several days earlier, a public memorial ceremony was held. Therefore, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, following other groups, respectfully appointed representative Luo Qinghua to go to Guangdong to pay respects to the spirit and attached a text saying: Since you passed away, times have changed several times. The stubborn and unyielding have deployed troops in the suburbs. The wind and cranes have spread throughout the city of Guangzhou. The soldiers are tired of war and return to the front line. The south gold and east arrows are used for national purposes. The world is clear, and the universe is peaceful. Relying on your legacy, we wash our hearts and change our faces. May your spirit rely on this and be glad. In the month of Xiaochun, the wind is gentle and the sun is shining. The pines and cypresses are lush, and the cemetery is eternally stable. The mountain of Xianshou is eternally loved by the masses. How can we repay? We offer the fruits of the field as a memorial. Please accept.

The Committee for Celebrating the 50th Birthday of Chairman Chiang, which purchased aircraft and presented them to the government, held its second preparatory meeting for the naming ceremony of the Zhongzheng Squadron aircraft at the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA yesterday at 5:00 PM. The French Government Decided to Reduce Tariffs; The Telephone Call from the Ambassador to France; From October 10, the Franc Devalued 117

The International Trade Bureau sent a letter to the national goods groups yesterday, saying: According to the instructions of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce No. 48863, the telegram from the Embassy in France on the 7th of this month stated that the French franc has devalued, and the French government has decided to reduce tariffs. From October 10, raw goods will be reduced by 25%, manufactured products will be reduced by 17%, and manufactured goods will be reduced by 15%. In addition, the exchange surcharge on our country will be reduced from 25% to 10%. In addition to waiting for the detailed report to arrive, we will issue another notice. It is imperative to inform you immediately and instruct the relevant merchants to be informed of this order, etc. In addition to sending a letter to the City Chamber of Commerce to forward it to the relevant merchants, it is appropriate to send a letter to your association for review and hope that you will forward it to the manufacturers under your jurisdiction.

Ministry of Finance Replied to Shanghai Grain Guild by Telegram: Bran Tax in Guangdong Province Has Been Abolished; Stop Collecting in Accordance with the Order at the End of August This Year 118

Regarding the case of the additional tax on bran in Guangdong Province, the national grain and oil cake industry had unanimously strived to abolish it, but there was no result. After the Guangdong Provincial Government obeyed the central government, the Shanghai Grain and Oil Cake Industry Guild and others telegraphed the Ministry of Finance again to request the abolition. The association received a telegram reply from the Ministry of Finance yesterday, stating that the collection has been stopped. The original telegram is recorded as follows: Shanghai Grain and Oil Cake Industry Guild, etc. After reviewing the previous request, we quickly ordered the current special commissioner of finance to abolish the harsh tax on bran in Guangdong Province as soon as possible in order to maintain domestic products, etc. The Ministry has already telegraphed the Guangdong Provincial Department of Finance for overall handling, and approved each case. According to the report submitted by Song Ziliang, the special commissioner of finance in Guangdong, on September 28 of this year, the letter from the Guangdong Provincial Department of Finance stated that the bran fee matters are under the jurisdiction of your department, and you should verify and handle it, etc. After checking the item of soybean bran, the collection of import surcharges was allocated to the construction of Sun Yat-sen University. The former Southwest Political Affairs Committee ordered the department to invite merchants to bid for the contract, collecting 25 cents of the ocean for each dan. Later, the tax was reduced by 15 cents of the ocean for each dan. In September of the 24th year, the Lian'an Company was approved to contract for 505,000 yuan of the ocean per year, for a period of one year. Later, the merchants were ordered to handle it until the end of the period, and the collection was stopped immediately. The period expired in August of this year. According to the report submitted by the contractor, it has been stopped until the end of August in accordance with the order. It is reasonable to submit a document to report for inspection, etc. In view of this, in addition to issuing instructions and sending telegrams, it is appropriate to send a telegram to inform you, Ministry of Finance, Hao Fu Seal.

More Than 5,000 People Paid Their Respects to Lu Xun's Remains Yesterday; Japan and Russia Both Sent Telegrams of Condolences; The Coffin Will Be Lowered This Afternoon and Buried Tomorrow Afternoon 119

After the news of the death of Lu Xun, a literary giant, spread, many telegrams of condolences came from all over the country, and more than 5,000 young men and women went to pay their respects to the remains yesterday. The body is scheduled to be placed in a coffin at 3:00 PM this afternoon and buried in the International Cemetery at 3:00 PM tomorrow afternoon. This morning until noon, it will still be available for all walks of life to pay their respects. The details of the situation are recorded as follows

A Glimpse of the Funeral Hall

The entrance to the funeral parlor is the registration office. The hall is set up in the downstairs hall. The four walls are full of elegiac couplets sent by all parties. There are two huge banners written in Esperanto and Roman characters, hanging on both sides. The mourning hall is at the west end of the hall. The entrance is decorated with flowers and banners, with the words "Loss of Our Good Teacher." The remains have been moved down from upstairs and placed horizontally in the hall. He is wearing a coffee-colored silk robe and looks lifelike, but his cheeks are thinner. His body is covered with a dark-colored brocade quilt, up to his chest. Behind it is a spiritual table, on which is enshrined an eight-inch portrait, all decorated with flowers, and bottles of flowers and wreaths given by various circles, piled up around. The windows in the room are hung with velvet curtains, the light is dark, and the air is solemn.

Elegiac Couplets from All Sides

The elegiac couplets are hung on all four walls. Here are a few excerpts: (1) Cai Yuanpei, "The writings are the most careful, not only the History of Chinese Novels. The last words are too painful, do not be a hollow literary man." (2) Cao Juren, "The literary world is bleak, a soldier wanders alone with a halberd. The high hill is now lonely, and the fragrant herbs are scattered and the pain remains in the spring." (3) Tang Tao, "Pain does not cry, bitterness does not cry, humiliation does not cry, what year is this year, two lines of tears flowed four months ago, who would have expected this time to be wet for the teacher again, words can be passed on, deeds can be passed on, teeth and eyes can be passed on, this old man is really old, for thirty years, he has opened up a bloody path, and it is up to future generations to shoulder this responsibility."

Visitors Crowd the Door

From yesterday morning to evening, those who went to pay their condolences and pay their respects to the remains were constantly on the way, totaling 102 groups and 5,298 mourners. Soong Ching Ling, He Xiangning, Soviet Ambassador to China Bogomolov, and Secretary E Shanyin, and well-known figures in the literary and art circles of various countries in Shanghai, all went to pay their condolences in person. There were more than 50 men's and women's school groups, and student associations from various places also sent representatives to attend. From 12:00 noon to 1:00 PM, there were many mourners, all of whom were male and female students, with schoolbags under their arms, coming in teams to pay their respects to the remains. After 4:00 PM, there were also many students. Two children, about ten years old, with black gauze on their arms, paid their respects in front of the spirit, their expressions solemn, which shows the respect of the intellectual circles for him.

Friendly Nations' Telegrams of Condolences

The news of his death was telegraphed to all parties by the funeral committee. Yesterday, many telegrams of condolences came from Japan and the Soviet Union. Here are a few excerpts: The Soviet Union Foreign Culture Association telegraphed: We were shocked and saddened to learn of the death of Mr. Lu Xun. Mr. Lu Xun was a great writer, and his sudden collapse is a loss to the literary world. It is hoped that you will restrain your grief and change your ways in order to rectify things. The Soviet Ambassador Bogomolov wrote in a letter to Mrs. Zhou: I was shocked and saddened to learn of the sudden death of Mr. Zhou. I specially express my condolences and hope that you will restrain your grief as much as possible. Yamamoto Saneshiko, the president of the Japanese Transformation Society, telegraphed: I am saddened to hear the news of Mr. Lu Xun's death. Yu Dafu telegraphed from Min: I was shocked to hear the news of Lu Xun's death and dared not believe it. I hope you will restrain your grief. Xin Dao, the president of Gyeongseong University in Korea, and Sawamura Yukio, the president of the Osaka Mainichi Shimbun, also sent telegrams of condolences.

Funeral Rites

Members of the funeral committee Cai Yuanpei, Soong Ching Ling, Uchiiyama Kanzo, Shen Junru, Mao Dun, and A. Smedley gathered on the second floor of the hall yesterday afternoon to discuss the funeral rites, etc. At that time, a press release was issued stating that: 1. The remains of Mr. Lu Xun will be placed in a coffin at 3:00 PM on October 21. From 9:00 AM to 2:00 PM on October 21, people from all walks of life will still be prepared to pay their respects to the remains and express their respect. 2. At 2:00 PM on October 22, the coffin will depart from the Guojiao Road International Funeral Home, and at 3:00 PM, it will be buried in the Hongqiao International Cemetery. 3. Because the International Cemetery is quite far away, people from all walks of life who depart from the International Funeral Home to attend the funeral are requested to prepare vehicles. 4. All condolences will be declined. Elegiac couplets, elegiac banners, and wreaths should be sent to the International Funeral Home on Guojiao Road and will be closed at noon on October 22. However, telegrams of condolence from all circles should be sent to Mao Dun, Literary Society, No. 2 Huacun, Jisi Feier Road, Shanghai, to the Lu Xun Funeral Committee.

Zhong and Shang Banks Entrusted by Shenxin to Establish Management Committee to Operate Factories No. 2 and No. 5; To Be Established After Rong Zongjing and Others Return to Shanghai from Wuxi; The Amount of Loan Will Be Determined According to Actual Needs 120

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, the Bank of China and the Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank have been entrusted by Shenxin Textile Company to operate its No. 2 and No. 5 factories, and a management committee will be established to preside over it. It will be announced after Rong Zongjing and others return to Shanghai from Wuxi, and textile production will begin. The details are recorded as follows:

Establish Management Committee to Preside Over Textile Production

Shenxin Factory No. 2 is located at No. 2 Yichang Road, with 56,744 yarn spindles and 7,140 thread spindles. Factory No. 5 is located at No. 1316 Huade Road, with 54,208 yarn spindles and 12,720 thread spindles. It has not been restored since it stopped work last year. Now, with the assistance of the Bank of China and the Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank in the Shenxin Factories No. 1, 2, 5 and 8 Syndicate, it has been decided that the Bank of China and the Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank will lend money to factories No. 2 and No. 5 again to start textile production. Shenxin Textile Company and the two banks signed a contract entrusting the management, and a management committee was established to preside over it. The members of the management committee are stipulated to be Pan Jiufen and Zhu Suwu from the Bank of China, and Zai Shouli, Li Yunhou and Tong Luqing from the Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank, and Rong Houren and Rong Hongyao from Shenxin Textile Company, a total of seven people.

The Amount of Loan Will Be Decided at Any Time

A reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency interviewed a bank member of the management committee last night. According to the talk, the management committee decided to announce its establishment after Rong Zongjing, the general manager of the company, and committee members Rong Hongyao and Rong Houren, returned to Shanghai from Wuxi. As for the factory directors of factories No. 2 and No. 5 and the date of commencement of work, a decision will be made after the management committee is established. The amount of the new loans from the Bank of China and the Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank will be determined according to needs. However, the management committee and the Shenxin Factories No. 1, 2, 5 and 8 Syndicate are not the same agency. The syndicate is the old creditor of the past, and the management committee is the new creditor of the Bank of China and the Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank. However, the Bank of China and the Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank are also the largest investors in the syndicate.

Yarn Market Turns Smoothly and Prices Soar; Shanghai's Yarn Inventory Is Nearly Exhausted; Factories and Exchange Warehouses Have Only 20,000 Bales; Spot Yarn Higher Than Standard Yarn Price Is Rare; Yarn Factories Open Day and Night Shifts to Rush Spinning; Cotton Prices Are Also Firm 121

After the yarn sales in various parts of our country turned smoothly, prices soared. The yarn inventories of various factories and exchange warehouses in Shanghai are about to be exhausted, totaling no more than 20,000 bales. The factories have opened day and night shifts to rush spinning. Although cotton is worth a bumper harvest, it is also firm due to the increase in yarn. A reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency learned the details from the yarn industry yesterday, which are recorded as follows:

Yarn Sales Turn Smoothly Suddenly

The reasons for the smooth yarn sales are: (1) The bumper harvest of agricultural products in various parts of our country has increased the people's purchasing power of yarn, and this is a universal phenomenon. All gangs have purchased a large amount, resulting in continuous yarn sales. (2) In the past, many yarn factories in Tianjin and Hankou stopped work for a long time, and at the same time, the factories in Shanghai unanimously reduced work, resulting in a reduction in production and a corresponding reduction in the quantity of supply. (3) The weaving industry in the inland of Jiangsu has turned better, and the cloth factories have all reported profits, so they purchased more raw materials. (4) Yarn sales in North China have been stagnant for a long time, but now they are suddenly very good.

Yarn Prices Soar

Yesterday, the highest standard yarn price for the October period was 238 yuan, a huge increase of 20 yuan in nearly a week. In the past, yarn prices were low in the near term and high in the distant term, with a difference of 10 yuan. Now, on the contrary, the near term is 15 yuan higher than the distant term. This is a phenomenon of actual firmness in the market price, not a speculative rise. The current rising trend of standard yarn is still very strong, but it has not exceeded the high point in the 18th year of the Republic of China. At that time, it was 183 taels, and the current shortage of goods is more serious than at that time.

Yarn Inventory Decreases

Shanghai's yarn inventory has always been above 100,000 bales in the past. It decreased to about 50,000 bales this summer, and then decreased again in the autumn. As of now, the total is 20,000 bales (including the yarn inventory in the exchange warehouse). As for the yarn inventory in the exchange warehouse, the most was on July 24 this year, totaling 36,890 bales. It gradually decreased to 36,335 bales on July 30, 33,345 bales on August 30, 22,020 bales on September 30, and 7,410 bales on October 19.

Factories Rush Spinning

The yarn inventory of various yarn factories in Shanghai is about to be exhausted, and the amount of yarn hoarding by various households has increased. In addition, due to the lack of spot yarn, the price has risen sharply, exceeding the standard yarn by more than 10 yuan, which is a rare phenomenon in the past. In the past, in January and February, the spot yarn sales were good, and the market price gradually increased. However, due to the situation, there were many short sellers on the exchange. Recently, the situation has eased, and the number of short sellers has decreased, so the yarn has also risen sharply. The Chinese yarn factories have all opened day and night shifts to spin yarn, because at the current price, the spun yarn can be profitable. As for the factories that have stopped work, such as Shenxin Factories No. 2 and No. 5, they have obtained the assistance of the Bank of China and the Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank to sort out the machinery and prepare to start work.

Flower Prices Are Also Firm

Although cotton in various parts of our country is worth a bumper harvest this year, its cotton price is also firm due to the increase in yarn. However, recently, the increase in yarn is generally greater than the increase in flowers. The phenomenon of expensive flowers and cheap yarn in the past is gradually changing, but it is still far from the constant difference between yarn and flowers in the past.

Eighty domestic goods manufacturers in this city, in view of the decision by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to hold a domestic goods exhibition, and with Chairman Wang Xiaolai and Vice Chairman Xu Xiaochu presiding over the proceedings, with considerable achievements, jointly produced and presented four plaques as a memento.

Currently, our country only has light industry, and in the future, we should also pay attention to heavy industry. British Export Credits Guarantee Department: Mr. Kirkpatrick 123

According to the "North-China Daily News," the British Export Credits Guarantee Department has appointed a representative to China, Mr. Kirkpatrick. Mr. Kirkpatrick will resign his seat as a Member of Parliament to come to Shanghai, and will work closely with Mr. Peel, the Commercial Counselor of the British Embassy in China, to handle all matters. Mr. Kirkpatrick will not submit any proposals himself, nor will he seek orders. He will only inquire about the financial and economic aspects of suggestions regarding the export of British goods to China. The guarantee of loans will be based purely on commercial principles. Therefore, the facilities granted as a result are neither existing nor intended to be a subsidy to British commerce. The British Embassy in China has sent a communique released yesterday in London to the "North-China Daily News," which is transcribed as follows: The Export Credits Guarantee Department officially announces that it has appointed Member of Parliament Mr. Kirkpatrick as its representative in China. Mr. Kirkpatrick will now vacate his parliamentary seat and temporarily work at the Department's London office before going to his office in China as soon as possible. Mr. Kirkpatrick will work closely with Mr. Peel, the Commercial Counselor of the British Embassy in China, to handle all matters. Judging from the number of guarantee constructions for the export of British goods to China recently received by the Department, it is clear that British manufacturers do not want to ignore opportunities in China. However, due to the rapid changes in the situation, coupled with the time and cost required for communication, the Department estimates that there are many obstacles to the risk of loans. The Department's appointment of Mr. Kirkpatrick to China is to have a representative on the spot to examine and consider the guarantee constructions proposed by British merchants, and to make any detailed investigations that may be necessary, and to engage in negotiations if necessary. Mr. Kirkpatrick will not submit any proposals himself, nor will he seek orders. He will only inquire about the financial and economic aspects of suggestions regarding the export of British goods to China that seem to be suitable for consideration under the British export credit plan. The export of British goods to China is often within the scope of the export credit plan. The decision to appoint him now only provides a mechanism to facilitate its implementation. The operation of this plan is purely based on commercial principles and not as a subsidy to British commerce, which has long been known. The Department is only concerned with British exporters, and there is no talk of negotiating loans or credit loans with the Chinese government.

Two Announcements from the Jianghai Customs 124

Zhu Changnian, Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs, and Baronsun, Commissioner of Customs, have issued the following notices regarding the deadline for claiming tax refund checks and the tax reduction for frozen duck exports:

Deadline for Claiming Tax Refund Checks

Announcement No. 1548 states: "According to an order from the Inspector General of Customs, all tax refund checks approved for issuance from January 1 to December 31, 1933, that have not yet been claimed must be claimed from the Customs before February 1, 1937. After the deadline, they will be canceled. Those who have already claimed the aforementioned checks but have not yet cashed them must cash them at the bank before January 31, 1937. After the deadline, they will also be invalidated. This order must be followed." Therefore, all merchants must be informed of this announcement.

Continued Tax Reduction for Frozen Duck Exports

Announcement No. 1549 states: "Regarding the tax reduction for frozen duck exports, the extension previously announced in Announcement No. 1470 on October 17 of last year is valid until the end of March of this year. Furthermore, according to an order from the Ministry of Finance, from October 1 of this year to March 31, 1937, all frozen duck exports will continue to be taxed at 5% ad valorem." This order must be followed. Therefore, all merchants must be informed of this announcement.
