The evening paper of the 19th reported that Mr. Lu Xun's remains would be moved to the Universal Funeral Home on Jiaozhou Road tomorrow for people to pay their respects. For such a giant in the Chinese national battle formation, we could not usually see him. Only after his death could he, with his final appearance, freely meet with the young people and social groups who admired him. With twelve million devout hearts, I got up very early on the morning of the 20th and rushed to the Universal Funeral Home to reverently pay respects to the remains of our old warrior and world star of the literary world.

I arrived at Jiaozhou Road at 8:30 in the morning. Because it was still early, the entrance of the Universal Funeral Home was quiet, and not many people had arrived yet. Upon entering, there were many greeters on both sides. After signing my name, I reverently stepped onto the memorial steps of the hall. Inside, there were very few people. The hall was decorated with flowers, grass, and pine trees. A dozen large wreaths were piled next to Mr. Lu Xun's portrait. A square face and a thick beard—this was the portrait of Mr. Lu Xun that we often saw in publications. On both sides of the portrait, there were two vases of fresh flowers with paper strips hanging down, on which were written: "Eternal rest to Teacher Lu Xun" and "Respectfully offered by twelve young people." In addition, there were huge wreaths from Mr. Lu Xun's only close friend during his lifetime, the Japanese businessman Kanzo Uchiyama, as well as Major General Yoshi of the Japanese military, Shen Yanbing, and others. This morning, half of the staff of Uchiyama Bookstore had been invited here to be greeters. Uchiyama had a special friendship with Lu Xun. This great friendship filled us with a great sense of respect.

The stairs were carpeted with soft carpets. I walked upstairs silently, gently, and solemnly. Mr. Lu Xun's remains were placed in a room on the west side. The bed was placed diagonally, and a chestnut-colored silk quilt quietly covered his remains. He lay quietly, his face extraordinarily thin. He had been ill for a long time. His thick beard was arranged untidily on his upper lip, and short beards also surrounded the lower ends of his cheeks. His eyes were closed quietly. Although thin, we could still recognize his vibrant style from the photos. This was the only giant of our era who influenced the entire cultural advancement front of China for more than a decade since the May Fourth Movement! I respectfully bowed to his remains. Many fresh flowers and wreaths were placed around the bed. I stood there, bewildered, and a wave of sorrow bit at my heart. I almost burst into tears. With what kind of heart should we mourn Mr. Lu Xun, this cultural giant and the only teacher of young people?

Several people were taking pictures. I was flustered and slowly retreated from his room. I went back to see him again. This was the first time I had seen this great cultural leader, and it was also the last time I would see him. No matter what, I could not suppress my sad heart!

After leaving the hall, I stood on the steps for a moment. By this time, more and more people were arriving. There were one or two hundred female students from a certain school, coming in a class. When I left the Universal Funeral Home, I predicted that more young people would come from afar, holding a devout heart, to pay their respects to the remains of this only giant of the literary world.

From Mr. Lu Xun's death, I thought of Maxim Gorky, the world's greatest writer who had passed away not long ago. When Gorky died, the Soviet people who lined up for miles to pay respects to his remains in Red Square numbered in the hundreds of thousands. However, the death of our era's only warrior, Mr. Lu Xun, only involved a few writers. He could not, after his death, allow more people to have the opportunity to pay their respects to him and express their condolences. However, his death would touch the hearts of every progressive young person in China, just like the death of Gorky.

Rent Collection 214

— Guo Ka

My mother went to the city to my sister's house, and my father also went out on business, leaving only me alone quietly reading in the house.

"Is Changgui home?"

Suddenly, the curtain opened, and a head covered with a broken reed hat peeked in and greeted me.

"Oh—" I raised my head blankly.

"A portion of rent grain."

"Oh."

So I put aside my book and found a small account book to temporarily perform the duties of a landlord.

The small account book had familiar words written by my father. I found the name mentioned by the person, looked at the words below the name, and said:

"One dou seven sheng five he?"

"That's about right, but I've already eaten quite a bit!"

He said hesitantly. I ignored him and stepped out.

He followed me to the grain storage room, placed the measuring tools, and untied the rope of the grain bag, while stammering again:

"Changgui, the wheat harvest is bad this year, and I've already eaten quite a bit."

This man was short and spoke with his face tilted up. His face seemed to tell people how foolish and obedient he was.

I habitually said:

"That won't do."

He mumbled even more:

"I'm afraid I'll eat even less and less. I swept it all together and brought it here today. I didn't dare eat any more rice for breakfast, just cooked some sticky porridge to drink!"

Although I was outwardly reserved, I was a little moved in my heart. I knew in what kind of sin I was living. As a result, much was still owed. This act of mine also moved him, and his eyes showed two beams of emotion, as if grateful that his little master was so kind!

At this moment, another person also came in carrying a bag of grain. This one was young, strong, and tall, with a sharp nose, as if a sign of untamedness.

He argued loudly with me, saying that the harvest was bad this year and he couldn't possibly pay in full.

According to the numbers in the small account book, after measuring each dou, the two people followed me to my father's room, watching me record the account, and reminding me as usual:

"Changgui, is it recorded in the account?"

I nodded, sitting quietly. They both took out their pipes to smoke. After smoking, the younger one put his pipe in the tobacco pouch and said to his companion:

"Let's go!"

"You go first, I'll stay for a while."

The younger one glanced at him and lifted the grain bag, leaving on his own.

The behavior of the one who remained intrigued me. I watched him quietly. He finally looked at me clumsily and said with an unnatural smile on the corner of his mouth:

"Changgui, do you have any cold pancakes (a type of food made with millet)? Give me a couple to eat. I only drank some thin porridge this morning, which wasn't filling enough, and I walked twenty li, so I'm terribly hungry!"

This sudden attack caught me a little off guard. I believe my expression was also unnatural. I quickly turned my head and said to a maidservant washing clothes in the yard:

"Are there any pancakes left? Give a few to this rent payer."

This maidservant was trained, she knew how to save things in front of the master. She made it up without thinking:

"That's terrible! Where are the pancakes? There weren't even enough to feed the dogs this morning."

I almost pleaded and commanded a few sentences before the person who had only drunk thin porridge in the morning received a few cold pancakes.

Looking at his satisfied gaze and tattered figure, I was deeply touched. I knew in what kind of sin I was raised!

Withered spring breeze and rain-soaked hair,

Who recognizes the former Han E adrift?

A song of sorrow in autumn breaks the heart.

Their love is deep and cannot be ignored.

Who knows that good things are always envied,

Endless sadness and evil storms arise.

But a beauty's heart is most difficult to grasp.

But see, jewelry and jade are dazzling, her heart is first drunk,

And she abandons her past affections into the blue sands.

How can she care for the oath and contract made in fragrant silk?

Alas, a foolish heart has no cure,

Alas, her fate is twisted, turning her into a moth in the orchids.

Calling out in grief on her sickbed, what can be done?

Suddenly crying, suddenly laughing,

New sorrows and old dreams blur together.

Thousands of ancient beauties have thin lives.

The lingering sound is entrusted to the Nanke dream.

Movie News

Jin Cheng Screens "Little Lingzi" Today 220

The style of national films mostly tends towards seriousness and composure, with few light and cheerful works. If there are any, "Little Lingzi" is the first. This film creates a unique style in Chinese cinema, breaking away from old tunes. It consistently adopts a lighthearted style, which has never been seen before. The director skills of Cheng Bugao, the screenwriting experience of Ouyang Yuqian, coupled with the deified expressions of Tan Ying and Zhao Dan, result in satisfactory achievements. The play depicts the story of a country girl who admires vanity, eventually being played by others. Pain is revealed in the lightness, and a bitter smile is contained in the humor. It is indeed a thought-provoking work. In addition to Tan Ying and Zhao Dan, the film also features Wang Xianqi, Pang Jianong, and Mei Xi as male actors, and Lu Luming, Shu Xiuwen, Ying Yin, and Green Leaf Peony as female actors. They complement each other well. It is produced by Star Film Company, and movie fans should be the first to see it.

"Reincarnated Hero" 221

Nanjing

"Blood Flower" to Be Released in Shanghai Soon 222

Originally titled "Three Girl Friends"

Regarding works composed using three characters, besides the Soviet film "Three Friends" which will be released soon, Dumas and Kipling have also written similar works in the past. This "Three Girl Friends" is also written using such a structure, but its protagonist is changed to female.

This film was well-received when it premiered in the United States, and was praised as the most emotional and stimulating of all Soviet films. It is the most emotional because the film is different from general Soviet films, as it depicts private life; it is the most stimulating because it uses the feelings of two people to express the emotions of the masses, and it never leaves the background of the masses.

It tells the story of three poor girls who made a living by singing when they were young. The process of their growing up coincided with major events such as the European War, the Revolution, and the Civil War. They participated in the Civil War, and one of the three inseparable girlfriends finally died tragically - using a tragedy to match the heroic ending, this film is even more powerful. It is now translated as "Blood Flower" and will be released soon at the Shanghai Grand Theater.
